***вспыхивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхивать.html>вспы́хивать</a> (4447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхнуть.html>вспы́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vspýxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхивать.html>вспы́хивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vspýxivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхнуть.html>вспы́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flash <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to briefly illuminate a scene</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to blaze up, to break out (of fire), to flare up</li>
<li>to blush, to flush</li></ol>

***вспыхнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхнуть.html>вспы́хнуть</a> (2907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пыхнуть.html>пыхну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pyxnútʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to puff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхнуть.html>вспы́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vspýxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхивать.html>вспы́хивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flash <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to briefly illuminate a scene</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to blaze up, to break out (of fire), to flare up</li>
<li>to blush, to flush
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “The Chorus Girl”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барыня.html>ба́рыня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вспыхнуть.html>вспы́хнула</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задрожать.html>задрожа́ло</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bárynja <b>vspýxnula</b>, i licó jejó zadrožálo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The lady <b>flushed</b> and her face quivered.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вспы́хивание</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vspýxivanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***вставать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вставать.html>встава́ть</a> (1088)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вставать.html>встава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand up, to get up, to rise</li>
<li>to rise <i>(sun)</i></li>
<li>to arise, to come up <i>(question)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подниматься.html>поднима́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podnimátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вставить.html>вста́вить</a> (3144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li>false, artificial <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a body part</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***встать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a> (367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">възстати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭzstati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">въз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз- / вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz- / vs-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восстать.html>восста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosstátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the Church Slavonic version of the prefix.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вставать.html>встава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand up, to get up, to rise</li>
<li>to rise <i>(sun)</i></li>
<li>to arise, to come up <i>(question)</i></li>
<li>to stop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подняться.html>подня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podnjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́женный</a> (6888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́женный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrevóžennyj</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrevóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́женный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrevóžennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>alarmed, anxious <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">experiencing alarm or anxiety; of a person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

***встревожить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́жить</a> (6888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trevóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrevóžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">встрево́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disturb</li>
<li>to worry, to trouble, to harass</li></ol>

***встрепенуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встрепенуться.html>встрепену́ться</a> (6810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">трепе-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepe-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встрепенуться.html>встрепену́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrepenútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rouse oneself, to start, <i>(bird)</i> to shake its wings, to open/spread its wings</li>
<li><i>(heart)</i> to throb, to beat faster</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">start</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздрогнуть.html>вздро́гнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzdrógnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">rouse oneself</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживиться.html>оживи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oživítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́титься</a> (1177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретить.html>встре́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrétitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́титься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrétitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to meet (with)</li>
<li>to come across, to run across</li>
<li>to encounter</li>
<li>to be found, to occur</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstréča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>meeting, encounter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ча</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rabóčaja <b>vstréča</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">workshop venue, business meeting, working-level meeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>date</li>
<li>reception</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаемый.html>встреча́емый</a> (1426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a> (1426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретить.html>встре́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrétitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrečátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретить.html>встре́тить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to meet, to encounter, to come across</li>
<li>to meet, to receive, to welcome</li>
<li>to celebrate
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>Но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a>? ― How did you celebrate the New Year? (lit. <i>How did you greet the New Year?</i>)</dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:неоднократно.html>Неоднокра́тно</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́л</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:неправильный.html>непра́вильное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ве</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:позвонить.html>позвонит</a>». </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ul></li>

</ol>

***встречаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a> (1114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrečátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́титься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to meet, to encounter, to come across (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взор.html>взо́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́тились</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ix vzóry <b>vstrétilisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">their eyes met</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднение.html>затрудне́ниями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstrečátʹsja</b> s zatrudnénijami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to encounter difficulties</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to see each other, to meet, to date
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rédko <b>vstrečátʹsja</b> s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see little of smb.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">částo <b>vstrečátʹsja</b> s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see a good deal of smb.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be found, to be met with, to occur, to happen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rédko <b>vstrečátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be uncommon, be rare in occurrence, be a rarity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> шотла́ндии <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дикий.html>ди́кие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v Šotlándii ješčó <b>vstrečájutsja</b> díkije kóški</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wild cats are still to be found in Scotland</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
